<script>
$jQ(function(){
	$jQ('.frnd_invite').click(function(){
		$jQ('.invitefrndCnt').show();
	});
	$jQ('.invitefrndCloseBtn').click(function(){
		$jQ('.invitefrndCnt').hide();
	});
	
});

function invite(){
	if(validateYRName('invite1','yrname') == true) {
		if(validateFRName('invite1','frname') == true) {
			var flag = validateEmail3('invite1','email');
			var url = "https://in.via.com/bdo?action1=FRINVT";
			var email = document.forms['invite1'].elements['email'].value;
			var toName = document.forms['invite1'].elements['frname'].value;
			var fromName = document.forms['invite1'].elements['yrname'].value;
			if(flag == true) {
				$jQ.ajax({
					type : "POST",
					url : url,
					data : 'email='+email+'&toName='+toName+'&fromName='+fromName ,
					success : function(data){
						if(data == 'true') {
							$jQ('.invitefrndCnt').hide();
							alert("Invitation Sent successfully");
						} else {
							alert("Invitation not Sent: please send again");
						}
					}
				}); 
			}
		}
	}
}

function validateYRName(formid,name) {
	var Name = document.forms[formid].elements[name].value;
	if(Name == null || Name == "" || Name.length < 1) {
		alert('Invalid Name');
	      return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	validateFRName('invite1','frname');
}

function validateFRName(formid,name) {
	var Name = document.forms[formid].elements[name].value;
	if(Name == null || Name == "" || Name.length < 1) {
		alert('Invalid Friends Name');
	      return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	validateEmail3('invite1','email');
}
function validateEmail3(formid,email) {
	   var reg = /^([A-Za-z0-9_\-\.])+\@([A-Za-z0-9_\-\.])+\.([A-Za-z]{2,4})$/;
	   var address = document.forms[formid].elements[email].value;
	   if(reg.test(address) == false) {
	      alert('Invalid Email Address');
	      return false;
	   } else {
		   return true;
	   }
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var CAPTCHA_UTIL = new function() {
	var count = 1;
	this.validateCaptcha = function() {
		var returnVal = false;
		var url = '/bdo?action1=CAPTCHA_VALID_ACTION';
		var captcha = document.getElementById('jcaptcha').value;
		$jQ.ajax({
			type : "POST",
			url : url,
			dataType: "text",
			async:false,
			data :  'jcaptcha='+captcha + '&image=jnumcaptcha',
			success : function(responseVal){
				
				if(responseVal == 'false') {
					document.getElementById('captchaValidMsg').innerHTML = "Please enter correct text";
					document.getElementById('captchaValidMsg').style.color="red";
					document.getElementById('captcha-img-div').innerHTML = "<img src='/captcha/jnumcaptcha.jpg?v="+count+"' /> &nbsp;&nbsp";
					document.getElementById('jcaptcha').focus();
					count++;
					returnVal = false;
				} else {
					document.getElementById('captchaValidMsg').innerHTML = "The text is Valid"; 
					document.getElementById('captchaValidMsg').style.color="green";
					document.getElementById('cpt_val').value = captcha;
					document.getElementById('vencpt').value = responseVal;
					count++;
					returnVal = true;
				}
			}
		});	
		return returnVal;
	}
	

	
	this.returnCaptchaParams = function() {
		return "&cpt_val="+document.getElementById('cpt_val').value+"&vencpt="+document.getElementById('vencpt').value;
	}
}


	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

SERVER_VARS._DOCTYPE = '';

function blinkText() {
	if(document.getElementById('blinkText')){	
 		document.getElementById('blinkText').style.visibility = (document.getElementById('blinkText').style.visibility=='visible')?'hidden':'visible';
 	} 
}
function showCountries() {
	$jQ('#otherCountries').toggle();
	var cur = 'INR';
	$jQ('#' + cur).hide();
}
function reloadPage(currency){
	var html = $jQ('<div>');
	var myForm = document.createElement("form");
	$jQ(myForm).attr("name","redirectForm").attr("method","post").attr("action","https://in.via.com/bdo");
	var formPrms = {};
	var myDiv = $jQ('<div>');
	for (var pnm in formPrms) {
		if(pnm != 'currency') {
			myDiv.append($jQ('<input>').attr({'type':'hidden', 'name':pnm, 'value': formPrms[pnm] }));
		}
	}
	myDiv.append($jQ('<input>').attr({'type':'hidden', 'name':'currency', 'value': currency }));
	myDiv.appendTo(myForm);
	document.body.appendChild(myForm);
	myForm.submit();
}

function showUserLoginBox(isFooterVisible){
	var b2cLoginURLiframe= 'https://localhost:8443' + '/membership/oauth2/login';
	var blockClassVal = 'blockB2cLogin';
	var iframe = $jQ('<iframe id="login_iframe">');

	if(isFooterVisible){
		b2cLoginURLiframe = b2cLoginURLiframe + '?showFooter=true';
	}
    iframe.attr({'src': b2cLoginURLiframe}).css({width: '100%',top: '25%','height':'345px','border':'none'});
    MODAL_PANEL.show(iframe, {title: '', blockClass : blockClassVal, close : true});
}
</script>

function showPromoVideos(num){
	var promoVideoPath = {
			1 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/B5V3DuqzR7E?rel=0',
			2 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/Mz7HAcczzec?rel=0',
			3 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/4c6PSEeDUdY?rel=0',
			4 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/42SsFnZhYOI?rel=0',
			5 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/Z4sqn38mRDY?rel=0',
			6 : 'http://www.youtube.com/embed/_SLuZzhUCmw?rel=0'		
	};
	var promoVideo = $jQ("<div>").css({'text-align':'center','border':'5px solid #595959'});
	var myPromoIFrame = $jQ('<iframe>').attr({'width':'650','height':'315','frameborder':'0','allowfullscreen':'true'});
	
	myPromoIFrame.attr('src',promoVideoPath[num]);
	promoVideo.append(myPromoIFrame);
	
	MODAL_PANEL.show(promoVideo, {title: 'Look what Via shot for you!', blockClass:'lgnRgBlk'});
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var curSelected="";
function assignAutoSuggestId(id) {
	var flag=true;
	var value='';
	if(curSelected=='src') {
		if(typeof(id.id)=='undefined') {
			value=id;
		} else {
			value=id.id;
		}

		document.getElementById('source').value=value;
		flag=false;
	}

	if(curSelected=='desti') {
		if(typeof(id.id)=='undefined') {
			value=id;
		} else {
			value=id.id;
		}
	
		document.getElementById('destination').value=value;
		flag=false;
	}
	if(flag){}
}	
function updateSourceValue(id){
	document.getElementById('source').value= id.options[id.selectedIndex].value;
}
function setSelectTextBox(val){
	curSelected=val;	
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var flightSearchTab;
$jQ(document).ready(function() {
	this.initFlt = function() {
		flightSearchTab = new FlightSearch("flightSearchForm",{hasInternational: false,hasAllCarrierClasses: false,validityStrength:"8",selectSingleAirline:false,is_international: null},{"customSubmit":false,"fphSearch":false});
	};
	setTimeout(this.initFlt,10);
	
		document.flightSearchForm.oneway[1].checked="checked";
		$jQ('#roundtripDiv').css('background-image','url("/static/img/general/input_select_on.png")');
		 selectRoundTrip();
	
	$jQ('#fphOptChk').attr({'checked':''});
});
function showHideDiv(){
	if(document.getElementById("domesinter")!=null && document.getElementById("domesinter").value=="domestic")
		document.getElementById("singleMultiCity").style.display="none";
	else if(document.getElementById("domesinter")!=null && document.getElementById("domesinter").value=="international"){
		document.getElementById("singleMultiCity").style.display="";
	}
}

function selectOneway() {
	document.flightSearchForm.returnType.value = "one-way";
	$jQ("#ReturnDiv, #EndDateDiv, #fphOptDiv, #fphHotelDiv").hide();
	$jQ("#EndDateDiv input").attr("disabled", "true");
	$jQ("#fphOptChk").attr("checked","");
	document.flightSearchForm.date2.value = "-Select-";
}
function selectRoundTrip() {
	document.flightSearchForm.returnType.value = "return";
	$jQ("#EndDateDiv input").removeAttr("disabled");
	$jQ("#ReturnDiv, #EndDateDiv, #fphOptDiv").show();
	$jQ("#fphOptChk").attr("checked","");
	document.flightSearchForm.date2.value = "-Select-";
}

function sr(val) {
	if(val == 0) {
		$jQ('input:radio[value=one-way]').click();
		$jQ('#onewayDiv').css('background-image','url("/static/img/general/input_select_on.png")');
		$jQ('#roundtripDiv').css('background-image','url("/static/img/general/input_select_off.png")');
	} else if (val == 1) {
		$jQ('input:radio[value=round-trip]').click();
		$jQ('#onewayDiv').css('background-image','url("/static/img/general/input_select_off.png")');
		$jQ('#roundtripDiv').css('background-image','url("/static/img/general/input_select_on.png")');
	}else if(val == 2){
		location.href="/bdo?action1=DFSRC&returnType=multi";
	}
}

function checkVal(radioButton){

if(radioButton.value=="single"){
	
		window.open("https://in.via.com/bdo?action1=FSRC&returnType=","_self" );
	
}else{
	
		window.open("https://in.via.com/bdo?action1=FSRC&returnType=multi","_self" );
	
}
}
function advanceSearchOptions(){	
	$jQ('#routingopts').toggleClass('u_invisible');
	$jQ('#customAirlineDiv').toggleClass('u_invisible');
	$jQ('#airlineClassdiv').toggleClass('u_invisible');
// 	var adSrch = $jQ('#advancesearch');
// 	var strS = (adSrch.val() =='+ Advanced Options')?"- Advanced Options":"+ Advanced Options"
// 	adSrch.val(strS);
}

function changeCity() {
	var selectedVal = $jQ("#destination").val();
	var city = areaMap[selectedVal];
	$jQ("#city").val(city);
}

function changeHotelCity(selectedVal){
	var city = airportCodeToMPCityMap[selectedVal];
	var cityName = airportCodeToMPCityNameMap[selectedVal];
	//$jQ("#city").val(city);
	$jQ('#city').html("<option selected value='" + city + "'>" + cityName  + "</option>");
	$jQ('#autocomplete_source').val(cityName);
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
$jQ(document).ready(function() {
	$jQ("#hldDealAltForm").validate({
		rules: {
			"email": {required: true, email: true}
		},
		messages: {
			"email": {required: "Please enter the email address", email: "Please enter a valid email address"},
			"mobile": {required: "Please enter your contact no.", mobile: "Please enter a valid mobile number"}
		}
	});
});
var HTLLEAD = new function() {
	this.show = function(htl) {
		$jQ("#hotelName").val(htl);
		
			MODAL_PANEL.show("#hldDealAltDiv", {title: 'Enter your budget and we will call you back', blockClass: 'lgnRgBlk'});
		
	}
	this.hide = function() {
		MODAL_PANEL.hide();
	}
	this.submitLead = function() {
		if (!$jQ("#hldDealAltForm").valid()) return false;
		
		AJAX_UTIL.asyncCall('/bdo',
			{params: $jQ("#hldDealAltForm").serialize(), scope: this, error: {}, success: {parseMsg:true, inDialog:true}});		
		this.trackLeadSubmit();			
	}
	this.trackLeadSubmit = function(){
		if($jQ("#lead_google_conversion").length > 0){
			$jQ("#lead_google_conversion").attr("src","https://in.via.com/bdo?action1=HOTEL_LEAD_GOOGLE_CONVERSION");
			//document.getElementById("lead_google_conversion").contentDocument.location.reload(true);
		}
		if(_gaq){
			_gaq.push(['PT._trackEvent', 'Hotels', 'Submit Lead', 'Query: []']);
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script>
	function showRecentSearches(){
		$jQ('.topSearches').toggleClass('u_invisible');
		if($jQ('.ftLinkArrow1').hasClass('a')){
			$jQ('.ftLinkArrow1').toggleClass('a',false);
			$jQ('.ftLinkArrow1').toggleClass('b',true);
		}else{
			$jQ('.ftLinkArrow1').toggleClass('a',true);
			$jQ('.ftLinkArrow1').toggleClass('b',false);
		}
	}
</script>

<script>
$jQ(function(){
	$jQ('.feedback').click(function(){
		MODAL_PANEL.show(".feedbackCnt", {title: "Feedback", blockClass: 'lgnRgBlk' });
		$jQ('.feedbackCnt').show();
	});
});

function clearFeedBackB2c(){
	$jQ('.clearFeedBack').val('');
	$jQ('#select_product').val('domestic_flight');
}

function submitFeedBack(){	
				if(validateFeedbackEmail('feedback1','email') == true) {
					if(validateFeedbackComment('feedback1','comm') == true) {
						var prod_type = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['select_product'].value;
						var fname = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['fname'].value;
						var lname = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['lname'].value;
						var email = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['email'].value;
						var phnum = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['phnum'].value;
						var fmnnum = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['fmnnum'].value;
						var sub = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['sub'].value;
						var comm = document.forms['feedback1'].elements['comm'].value;
						var url = "https://in.via.com/bdo?action1=FDBCK";
						$jQ.ajax({
							type : "POST",
							url : url,
							data : 'prod_type='+prod_type+'&fname='+fname+'&lname='+lname+'&email='+email+'&phnum='+phnum+'&fmnnum='+fmnnum+'&sub='+sub+'&comm='+comm+'&fromjsp=feedback_viacom' ,
							success : function(data){
								if(data == 'true') {
									MODAL_PANEL.hide();
									clearFeedBackB2c();
									alert('Thanks for the Feedback. Your Feedback successfully reported.');
								} else {
									alert('Sending FeedBack failed. Please send it again');
								}
							}
						}); 
					}
				}
}

function validateFName(formid,name) {
	var Name = document.forms[formid].elements[name].value;
	if(Name == null || Name == "" || Name.length < 1) {
		alert('Invalid First Name');
	      return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	validateLName('feedback1','lname');
}

function validateLName(formid,name) {
	var Name = document.forms[formid].elements[name].value;
	if(Name == null || Name == "" || Name.length < 1) {
		alert('Invalid Last Name');
	      return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	validateFeedbackEmail('feedback1','email');
}

function validateFeedbackEmail(formid,email) {
	   var reg = /^([A-Za-z0-9_\-\.])+\@([A-Za-z0-9_\-\.])+\.([A-Za-z]{2,4})$/;
	   var address = document.forms[formid].elements[email].value;
	   if(reg.test(address) == false) {
	      alert('Invalid Email Address');
	      return false;
	   } else {
		   return true;
	   }
	   //validatePhNum('feedback1','phnum');
}

function validatePhNum(formid,num) {
	var Num = document.forms[formid].elements[num].value;
	if(isNaN(Num) || Num.length > 12 || Num.length < 10 ) {
		alert('Invalid Phone Number');
	      return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	validateFeedbackComment('feedback1','comm'); 
}

function validateFeedbackComment(formid,comm) {
	var Comm = document.forms[formid].elements[comm].value;
	if(Comm.length < 1) {
		alert('Please enter Comments');
		return false;
	} else if(Comm.length > 600) {
		alert('Comment can only be of maximum 600 characters');
		return false;
	} else {
		return true;
	}
	$jQ('.myFeedbackForm').submit();
}

var showHotelDest = (function (){
	var count = 1;	
	return function(){
		if((count)%2 == 0){$jQ(".ftLinkArrow").css("backgroundPosition","0 85px");}else{$jQ(".ftLinkArrow").css("backgroundPosition","0 33px")}
		$jQ("#featuredHotelDest").toggle();
		count++;
	}
})();
</script>
